Accenture&#8217;s management believes that this information provides meaningful additional information regarding the company&#8217;s liquidity. </span></div><div style="padding-left:72pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.85pt">Percentage changes in revenues and bookings on a local currency basis. Financial results in local currency are calculated by restating current period activity into U.S. dollars using the comparable prior year period&#8217;s foreign currency exchange rates. This approach is used for all results where the functional currency is not the U.S. dollar. Accenture&#8217;s management believes that information regarding changes in its revenues and bookings that excludes the effect of fluctuations in foreign currency exchange rates facilitates meaningful comparison of its revenues. </span></div><div style="padding-left:72pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.85pt">Diluted earnings per share, effective tax rate, income before income taxes, income tax expense, and net income excluding gains on an investment. Accenture&#8217;s management believes that information regarding the effect of the investment gains facilitates an understanding as to the impacts of the investment and the company&#8217;s financial performance.</span></div><div style="margin-top:5pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Reconciliations of these non-GAAP financial measures to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP are included in the news release. While Accenture&#8217;s management believes that this non-GAAP financial information is useful in evaluating Accenture&#8217;s operations, this information should be considered as supplemental in nature and not as a substitute for the related financial information prepared in accordance with GAAP.</span></div><div style="margin-top:14pt"><span <title>Document</title></head><body><div id="i36890e0811074521b50d7369564979e1_1"></div><div style="min-height:58.5pt;width:100%"><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div><div style="text-align:right"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Exhibit 99</font></div><div style="text-align:right"><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-right:-4.5pt;text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Accenture Reports Very Strong Fourth-Quarter and Full-Year Fiscal 2021 Results </font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">-- For the fourth quarter, revenues increase 24% in U.S. dollars and 21% in local currency, to $13.4 billion&#59; EPS increase 11% to $2.20 from $1.99 last year, which included $0.29 in gains on an investment&#59; EPS increase 29% from adjusted EPS of $1.70 last year -- </font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">-- For full fiscal year, revenues are a record $50.5 billion, an increase of 14% in U.S. dollars and 11% in local currency&#59; operating margin expands 40 basis points to 15.1%&#59; EPS increase 16% to $9.16 from $7.89 last year, which include $0.36 and $0.43, respectively, in gains on an investment&#59; excluding these gains, adjusted EPS increase 18% to $8.80 in fiscal 2021 from $7.46 in fiscal 2020 --  </font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">-- Free cash flow is $2.2 billion for fourth quarter and $8.4 billion for full year -- </font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">-- New bookings are $15.0&#160;billion for fourth quarter and a record $59.3&#160;billion for full year, a 20% increase in U.S. dollars over full-year fiscal 2020 new bookings --</font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">-- Company increases quarterly cash dividend 10%, to $0.97 per share&#59; Board of Directors approves $3.0 billion of additional share repurchase authority --</font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">-- For fiscal year 2022, Accenture expects revenue growth of 12% to 15% in local currency and GAAP diluted EPS of $9.90 to $10.18, an increase of 13% to 16% from adjusted EPS for fiscal 2021 --</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">NEW YORK&#59; Sept. 23, 2021 &#8212; Accenture (NYSE&#58; ACN) reported financial results for the fourth quarter and full fiscal year ended Aug. 31, 2021. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">For the fourth quarter</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">, revenues were $13.4&#160;billion, an increase of 24% in U.S. dollars and 21% in local currency compared with the fourth quarter of fiscal 2020.&#160;Diluted earnings per share were $2.20, an 11% increase from $1.99 last year, which included $0.29 in gains on an investment. Diluted EPS increased 29% from adjusted EPS of $1.70 for the fourth quarter last year. Operating margin for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2021 was 14.6%, an expansion of 30 basis points from the fourth quarter of fiscal 2020. Operating cash flow was $2.4&#160;billion and free cash flow was $2.2 billion. New bookings were $15.0&#160;billion.   </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">For the full fiscal year</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">, revenues were $50.5&#160;billion, an increase of 14% in U.S. dollars and 11% in local currency compared with fiscal 2020. Diluted earnings per share increased 16% to $9.16 from $7.89 last year, including gains on an investment of $0.36 and $0.43, respectively. Excluding these gains, adjusted diluted EPS for fiscal 2021 were $8.80, an 18% increase from $7.46 in fiscal 2020. Operating margin for fiscal 2021 was 15.1%, an expansion of 40 basis points. Operating cash flow for fiscal 2021 was $9.0 billion and free cash flow was $8.4&#160;billion. New bookings were a record $59.3&#160;billion. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Julie Sweet, Accenture&#8217;s Chair &#38; CEO, said, &#8220;We are very proud of our outstanding fiscal 2021 financial performance, reflecting growth significantly above the market and strong momentum heading into fiscal 2022. Our results reflect the dedication and hard work of our 624,000 incredible people, who are laser-focused on creating tangible value for our clients, innovating with our ecosystem, and being the trusted partner of choice on our clients&#8217; transformation journeys.&#160;We delivered these results while investing in our people and in the capabilities our clients need, now and in the future, and at the same time making progress on our sustainability goals &#8212; from progress in inclusion and diversity, to the use of renewable energy now at 50% </font></div><div style="height:36pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:58.5pt;width:100%"><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">across the globe, to supporting our communities during these challenging times.&#160;We measure our success by this 360&#176; value creation.&#8221;&#160;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%;text-decoration:underline">Financial Review</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Fourth Quarter Fiscal 2021</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Revenues for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2021 were $13.42 billion, compared with $10.84&#160;billion for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2020, an increase of 24% in U.S. dollars and 21% in local currency. Revenues for the quarter reflect a foreign-exchange impact of approximately positive&#160;3%, compared with the positive 4% impact previously assumed. Adjusting for the actual foreign-exchange impact, the company&#8217;s guided range for quarterly revenues was approximately $13.0 billion to $13.4 billion. Accenture&#8217;s fourth-quarter fiscal 2021 revenues were slightly above this adjusted range.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Wingdings',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.25pt">Consulting revenues were $7.31&#160;billion, an increase of 29% in U.S. dollars and 25% in local currency compared with the fourth quarter of fiscal 2020.</font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Wingdings',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.25pt">Outsourcing revenues were $6.11 billion, an increase of 19% in U.S. dollars and 16% in local currency compared with the fourth quarter of fiscal 2020.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">GAAP diluted EPS for the fourth quarter were $2.20, an increase of $0.21 or 11% from $1.99 for the fourth quarter last year, which included gains on an investment of $219 million, pre-tax, or $0.29 per share. EPS for the quarter increased $0.50, or 29%, from adjusted EPS of $1.70 for the fourth quarter last year. The $0.50 increase in EPS on an adjusted basis reflects&#58; </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Wingdings',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.25pt">a $0.46 increase from higher revenue and operating results&#59; </font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Wingdings',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.25pt">a $0.10 increase from a lower effective tax rate&#59; and  </font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Wingdings',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.25pt">a $0.01 increase from a lower share count&#59;   </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">partially offset by</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Wingdings',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.25pt">a $0.07 decrease from higher non-operating expenses.   </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Gross margin (gross profit as a percentage of revenues) for the fourth quarter was 33.3%, compared with 31.8% for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2020. Selling, general and administrative (SG&#38;A) expenses for the fourth quarter were $2.51&#160;billion, or 18.7% of revenues, compared with $1.90&#160;billion, or 17.5% of revenues, for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2020. </font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> </font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Operating income for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2021 was $1.96&#160;billion, or 14.6% of revenues, compared with $1.54 billion, or 14.3% of revenues, for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2020. Operating margin for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2021 expanded 30 basis points.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The company&#8217;s effective tax rate for the fourth quarter was 25.0%, compared with 26.8% for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2020. Excluding the impact of gains on an investment, the effective tax rate was 28.4% for the fourth quarter last year.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Net income for the quarter was $1.44 billion, compared with $1.31&#160;billion for the fourth quarter of fiscal 2020. Excluding the $185 million after-tax impact of gains on an investment, net income was $1.12 billion for the fourth quarter last year. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="height:36pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:58.5pt;width:100%"><div style="text-align:center"><font><br></font></div></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Operating cash flow for the fourth quarter was $2.44&#160;billion, and property and equipment additions were $236&#160;million. Free cash flow, defined as operating cash flow net of property and equipment additions, was $2.20&#160;billion. For the same period of fiscal 2020, operating cash flow was $3.16&#160;billion, property and equipment additions were $189&#160;million, and free cash flow was $2.97&#160;billion.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Days services outstanding, or DSOs, were 38 days at Aug. 31, 2021, compared with 35 days at Aug. 31, 2020. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Accenture&#8217;s total cash balance at Aug. 31, 2021 was $8.2&#160;billion, compared with $8.4&#160;billion at Aug. 31, 2020.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">New Bookings</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">New bookings for the fourth quarter were $15.0&#160;billion, an increase of 7% in U.S. dollars and 5% in local currency from the fourth quarter last year.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Wingdings',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.25pt">Consulting new bookings were $8.0&#160;billion, or 53% of total new bookings. </font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Wingdings',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.25pt">Outsourcing new bookings were $7.1&#160;billion, or 47% of total new bookings. </font></div><div style="padding-left:18pt"><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Revenues by Geographic Market </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Revenues by geographic market for the fourth quarter were as follows&#58; </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Wingdings',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.25pt">North America&#58; $6.39&#160;billion, an increase of 23% in U.S. dollars and 22% in local currency compared with the fourth quarter of fiscal 2020. </font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.25pt">Europe&#58; $4.30&#160;billion, an increase of 26% in U.S. dollars and 18% in local currency compared with the fourth quarter of fiscal 2020. </font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font 21% in local currency compared with the fourth quarter of fiscal 2020. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Revenues by Industry Group</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font </font></div><div style="padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Wingdings',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.25pt">a $0.09 increase from a lower effective tax rate&#59; if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
